        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer865413965" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17015715163724761781">This book is part of Lynsay Sands "Argeneau Vampire" series and I have been hooked since I read the first one. This one is pretty good but I was having a bit of trouble with the time-line with this one but with that aside I loved both Marcus Notte and Basha Argeneau in this one. You will meet some of the others from the other books and it's always nice to revisit with old friends.. ;-)<br/><br/>Now some of the other reviews have found this one to be a bit "darker" than the others books in this series and </span>
  <span id="freeText17015715163724761781" style="display:none">This book is part of Lynsay Sands "Argeneau Vampire" series and I have been hooked since I read the first one. This one is pretty good but I was having a bit of trouble with the time-line with this one but with that aside I loved both Marcus Notte and Basha Argeneau in this one. You will meet some of the others from the other books and it's always nice to revisit with old friends.. ;-)<br /><br />Now some of the other reviews have found this one to be a bit "darker" than the others books in this series and maybe even have a bit less humor and they could be right but I find this book to be a good read<br /><br /><i>For Basha Argeneau, anything is better than facing her estranged family. Even hiding out in sweltering southern California. But when a sexy immortal in black shows up determined to bring her back to the clan, she'll do anything to keep far, far away from the past she can't outrun.<br /><br />Marcus Notte isn't here to play games—especially not with someone as crazy as the infamous blonde. Asked by Lucian Argeneau to bring her back for questioning, Marcus is determined to carry out Lucian's request—no matter how the seductive little mind-reading vamp feels about it.<br /><br />Basha doesn't mind fighting fire with fire, especially with a hot immortal involved. But if he wants to take her away, he'll have to catch her first . . .</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="17015715163724761781" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/866287153?book_show_action=true">Feb 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/5707336-michelle">Michelle</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer866287153" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15066229686680954764">Twenty books in to the <i>Argeneau</i> series and I enjoyed this every bit as much as book one. Because this is such a long standing series and there are so many interwoven characters, I wouldn’t actually recommend starting with this book. Basha has been hiding for hundreds of years, most recently as a fortune teller in a circus. She’s been trying to hide for years from the Argeneau family, afraid of the power they wield. Marcus is assisting in location a possible rogue vampire and is trying to determi</span>
  <span id="freeText15066229686680954764" style="display:none">Twenty books in to the <i>Argeneau</i> series and I enjoyed this every bit as much as book one. Because this is such a long standing series and there are so many interwoven characters, I wouldn’t actually recommend starting with this book. Basha has been hiding for hundreds of years, most recently as a fortune teller in a circus. She’s been trying to hide for years from the Argeneau family, afraid of the power they wield. Marcus is assisting in location a possible rogue vampire and is trying to determine what Basha could possibly know. They have so many secrets to hide from each other and because neither can read the other, the battle to learn the truth becomes hot and heavy. I really love knowing that I can pick up a novel from Ms. Sands and enjoy myself. She writes characters with humor and gives a story that not only draws you in but offers the sweet and sexy of a good romance read. Can’t wait to read what comes next!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15066229686680954764" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14645683-enzo?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14645683-enzo?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer898108987" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10931825713954450243">Yes the love of the fangs once again pulls me back to the Argeneau series. This particular story in the series is a bit darker than most. But it still includes those brilliant touches of laughter and levity that make it so good. For those in the know, Lynsay Sands has one of the best Vampire/Paranormal series out there. But most just look at it as a romance novel. The series started that way but it has now branched into very interesting themes. You have the romance part of the equation but you a</span>
  <span id="freeText10931825713954450243" style="display:none">Yes the love of the fangs once again pulls me back to the Argeneau series. This particular story in the series is a bit darker than most. But it still includes those brilliant touches of laughter and levity that make it so good. For those in the know, Lynsay Sands has one of the best Vampire/Paranormal series out there. But most just look at it as a romance novel. The series started that way but it has now branched into very interesting themes. You have the romance part of the equation but you also have Rogues and now a serious move to No-Fangers. You can also foresee a future of the series moving to Europe or even Asia following the Argeneau-Notte families. <br /><br />Who is it recommended to: Romance readers will find it good and entertaining. Vampire readers depending if they like the horror/gore or will they move to urban paranormal stories. <br /><br />So take a look at the series I promise that you'll end up reading more than one and enjoying it. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10931825713954450243" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('CUCOKog2QS7JhbEduVHBuLDb8tRPYy1IaxLoqlDQe2avXnbrh77EKHFHS41n/mSHb45LqeJZyZA2y+NFK+/IVw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('trGuii8IrScQboasRI1tmfUi71KXN6BkTJHovZgZ37MQr1ZLIIAoIaisfDyaIsimKndWLzoNRLwRSONS4yZsgg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer18236886535059888626">LYNSAY SANDS is the nationally bestselling author who is known for her hysterical historicals as well as the popular Argeneau/Rogue Hunter vampire series. With her witty and charming personality, Sands describes books as, “Waking dreams or stories, tales to amuse, entertain and distract us from everyday life.” She’s been writing stories since grade school and considers herself incredibly lucky to </span>
  <span id="freeText18236886535059888626" style="display:none">LYNSAY SANDS is the nationally bestselling author who is known for her hysterical historicals as well as the popular Argeneau/Rogue Hunter vampire series. With her witty and charming personality, Sands describes books as, “Waking dreams or stories, tales to amuse, entertain and distract us from everyday life.” She’s been writing stories since grade school and considers herself incredibly lucky to be able to make a career out of it. Her hope is that readers can get away from their everyday stress through her stories, and if there are occasional uncontrollable fits of laughter, that’s just a big bonus. Visit her official website at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.lynsaysands.net">www.lynsaysands.net</a>.<br /><br /></span>
